<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function ReturnFromPopup__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(e) {
        var dataViewSettings = {
            GridHeight: '500',
            AdjustGridHeightOnResize: 'True',
            VerticallyScrollable: 'True',
            IsGridEditable: 'false'
        };

        var urls = {
            ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault',
            ResetNamedGridSettingsSave: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveNamedGridSetting',
            ExistsInSession: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/NamedGridSettingseExistInSession',
            GetGridUserSettingsView: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetUserGridSettingsView',
            GetNamedGridSettings: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetNamedGridSettings',
            DeleteNamedGridSetting: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteNamedGridSetting',
            SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault',
            RemoveMyDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RemoveMyDefault',
            Apply: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyNamedGridSettings'
        };

        var msgs = {
            Success: "Record saved successfully.",
            Delete: "Record deleted successfully.",
            ConfirmDelete: "Confirm Delete",
            DeleteSelectedRecords: "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?"
        };

        UserGridSettingsMenuReturn('/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', e, 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView', urls.GetNamedGridSettings, dataViewSettings, urls.Apply,
                                    function (e) {
                                        UserGridSettingsMenuOnSelect(e, '/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView', dataViewSettings, urls, msgs)
                                    });
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        UpdataNamedGridSettingsMenu('/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView', '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetNamedGridSettings',
            function (e) {
                UserGridSettingsMenuOnSelect(e, '/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView',
                {
                    GridHeight: '500',
                    AdjustGridHeightOnResize: 'True',
                    IsGridEditable: 'false'
                },
                {
                    ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault',
                    ResetNamedGridSettingsSave: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveNamedGridSetting',
                    ExistsInSession: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/NamedGridSettingseExistInSession',
                    GetGridUserSettingsView: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetUserGridSettingsView',
                    GetNamedGridSettings: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetNamedGridSettings',
                    DeleteNamedGridSetting: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteNamedGridSetting',
                    SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault',
                    RemoveMyDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RemoveMyDefault',
                    Apply: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyNamedGridSettings'
                },
                {
                    Success: "Record saved successfully.",
                    Delete: "Record deleted successfully.",
                    ConfirmDelete: "Confirm Delete",
                    DeleteSelectedRecords: "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?"
                })
            });
    });

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView', GridHeight: '500', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '500', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').val(), 
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',

                isEditable: false
            },

                $('#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {

            }
        });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $("#btnPreviewNetPay__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();


        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) return;
        var options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/PreviewNetPay", data: { selectedId: selectedRowIds }, type: "POST" };


        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupPayrollPreviewNetPay')
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetHeight('90%')
       .SetWidth(1170)
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetTitle('Preview Net Pay')

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    $("#btnRollover__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupwindowRolloverDeduction')
                .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/Rollover" })
                .SetHeight('20%')
                .SetWidth(550)
                .SetIsModal(true)
                .SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
                .SetTitle('Rollover Deduction Sets')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "RolloverDeductionSets", null);

    });

        e.preventDefault();


        if (!$("#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView")
              .ValidateDataViewGridSelection(false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation."))
            return;
        CopyDeductionSetMessage("divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/CopyDeductionSetMessage', '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/CopyDeductionSet', "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DetailPopup", 'Deduction Details', "Confirm")


    });



    function ReloadPage() {
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/Manage";// + "?EmployeeId=" + GetEmployeeId()
    }

    function RefreshOnProcessRolloverDeductions(empId) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        var key = 'PayrollEmployeeDeduction';
        $("#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/ApproveDeductionSet',
                         { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, empId: empId },
                    key, function (result) {
                        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    $("#btnApprove__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView")
                .ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
            return;

        var arr = selectedRowIds.split(',');
        var empId = arr[0].split('~')[0];

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/VerifyDeductionSet',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (!result) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Error", "Please select deduction set with new status to perform this operation", null);
                    return;
                }
                else {

                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnProcessRolloverDeductions(empId); });
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);


                }
            }
        });

    });

    $("#btnAddScreen__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/CreateDeductionSet" + "?EmployeeId=0";

    });

    $("#btnAdd__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/CreateDeductionSetPopup", data: { EmployeeId: 0 }, type: "POST" };
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupWindowDeductions')
      .SetContent(options)
      .SetHeight('90%')
      .SetWidth(1050)
      .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
      .SetIsModal(true)
      .SetTitle('Deduction Details')

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    });

    $("#btnEditScreen__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        //debugger;
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/Detail" + "/" + selectedRowIds;

    });


    function EditEmployeeDeductionScreen(id) {
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditEmployeePayrollDeductionScreen(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditEmployeePayrollDeductionScreen(id,aptaDataViewSelection)
    {
        var options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DetailPopup", data: { id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, sourceDataView: "EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView" }, type: "POST" };
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupWindowDeductions')
        .SetContent(options)
        .SetHeight('90%')
        .SetWidth(1050)
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetIsModal(true)
        .SetTitle('Deduction Details')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    }

    $("#btnEdit__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divEmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditEmployeePayrollDeductionScreen(0, aptaDataViewSelection)
        }
    });

    function IsNewDeductionSet() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        //
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();

        for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
            if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds) {

                var DeductionSetStatus = gridData[i].DeductionSetStatus;

                if (DeductionSetStatus == "New" || DeductionSetStatus == "New Copy") {
                    return true;
                }
                break;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    $("#btnDelete__EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();


        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        //debugger;
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        if (!IsNewDeductionSet()) {
            ShowOkDialog("Error", "You can not delete a deduction set that is not in the New or New Copy status.", null);
            return;

        }
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected record?", DeleteDeductionSet);

    });
    function DeleteDeductionSet() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DeleteDeductionSet" + "/" + selectedRowIds;
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">


        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function ShowAptaFundJobQueueNotification(type, data, title) {
            FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.ShowJobQueueNotification(data, title)
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "")
                        ShowAptaFundJobQueueNotification("jobqueue", result.TempData, result.Message);
                    else
                        HideAptaFundNotification();
                }
            });
        }

        function HideAptaFundNotification() {
            FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.ShowJobQueueNotification(null, null)
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        FINSUI.JobQueueNotifications.SetBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action")
        FINSUI.JobQueueNotifications.htmlElement = $("#AptaFundNotification")
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

        });


    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>
    var employeeId = '495';
    var changeNumber = '37';
    var cycleId = '4';

    function GetStateWitholdingView() {
        if (changeNumber === "") {
            return;
        }
        var state = $("#StateCode").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
        var id = employeeId + '~' + cycleId + '~' + changeNumber;
        var data = { id: id, state: state };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/StateWithholding",
            data: data,
            dataType: 'html',
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null) {
                    $("#State").html(result);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {

            }
        });
    }

    function OnGTLCoverageTypeChange() {
        switch ($("#GTLCoverageType").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
            case "F":
                {
                    $("#GTLFactor").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
                    $('label[for="GTLFactor"]').hide();
                    $("#GTLFactor").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue('');

                    $("#GTLDistribution").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="GTLDistribution"]').show();

                    $("#GTLCoverage").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(true);
                    $('label[for="GTLCoverage"]').show();

                    $("#GTLAdditionalAmount").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
                    $('label[for="GTLAdditionalAmount"]').hide();
                    $("#GTLAdditionalAmount").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue('');

                    break;
                }
            case "P":
            case "M":
                {
                    $("#GTLFactor").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(true);
                    $('label[for="GTLFactor"]').show();
                    $("#GTLDistribution").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(false)
                    $('label[for="GTLDistribution"]').hide();

                    $("#GTLCoverage").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
                    $('label[for="GTLCoverage"]').hide();
                    $("#GTLCoverage").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue('');

                    $("#GTLAdditionalAmount").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(true);
                    $('label[for="GTLAdditionalAmount"]').show();

                    break;
                }
            default:
                {
                    break;
                }

        }
    }

    var loadTabFA = true;
    var loadTabPercenage = true;
    var loadTabDD = true;
    var loadTabOCG = true;

    function onActivate(e) {
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        var activeTabText = $("#tabstrip").data("FINSUITabStrip").GetActiveTabText();

        if (activeTabText == 'Fixed Amount') {
            var gridAdd = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadTabFA) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView();
                loadTabFA = false;

            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", "PayrollEmployeeDeduction", "EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabText == 'Percentage') {
            var gridPercentage = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentPercentageDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadTabPercenage) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmpPyDedAssignmentPercentageDataView();
                loadTabPercenage = false;

            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", "PayrollEmployeeDeduction", "EmpPyDedAssignmentPercentageDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabText == 'Direct Deposit') {
            var gridDD = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadTabDD) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView();
                loadTabDD = false;

            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", "PayrollEmployeeDeduction", "EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabText == 'Override Group Cap') {
            var gridDD = $("#PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadTabOCG) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView();
                loadTabOCG = false;

            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", "PayrollEmployeeDeduction", "PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView");
        }

    }
</script>

    $(document).ready(function () {

            var Id = $("#hdnMaskedValue_DeductionAssignmentSSNLabel").val();

                        else {
                            $("#lblVendorTaxIdValue_DeductionAssignmentSSNLabel").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        $("#showMaskedValue_DeductionAssignmentSSNLabel").text(response.buttonText);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });


</script>

                alert("Settings__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView').click(function () {

        //refreshing source grid data

        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

            cache: false,

            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                InitializeGrid___EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();

                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView");

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView", "1");
                    GridSetSelectedItemsOn("EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView", "");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    $("#btnCancel__PayrollEmployeeDeduction").click(function (e) {

    $("#btnPreviewNetPay__PayrollEmployeeDeduction").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();

        var options = { url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/PreviewNetPay", data: { selectedId: '495' + "~" + '4' + "~" + '37' }, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject('popupPayrollPreviewNetPay')
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetHeight('90%')

    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails", "PayrollEmployeeDeduction", null);

    $(document).ready(function () {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView", "PayrollEmployeeDeduction", "EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView");
        if (changeNumber &gt; 0) {
            $("#GTLFactor").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
            $('label[for="GTLFactor"]').hide();
            var isReadOnly = 'False';
            if(isReadOnly == 'False'){
                switch ($("#GTLCoverageType").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                    case "F":
                        {
                            $("#GTLFactor").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
                            $('label[for="GTLFactor"]').hide();


                            $("#GTLCoverage").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(true);
                            $('label[for="GTLCoverage"]').show();

                            $("#GTLAdditionalAmount").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
                            $('label[for="GTLAdditionalAmount"]').hide();

                            break;
                        }
                    case "P":
                    case "M":
                        {
                            $("#GTLFactor").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(true);
                            $('label[for="GTLFactor"]').show();

                            $("#GTLDistribution").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                            $('label[for="GTLDistribution"]').hide();

                            $("#GTLCoverage").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetVisible(false);
                            $('label[for="GTLCoverage"]').hide();
                            break;
                        }
                    default:
                        {
                            break;
                        }
                }
            }
            GetStateWitholdingView();

        }

        if ('37' == 0) {
            $('#divEmployee').show();
            if ('495' == '0')
                $("#DeductionEmployeeId").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue('');
        }
        else {
            $('#divEmployee').hide();
        }

    });

    function EditDirectDepositDetail(CycleId, DepositId, ChangeNumber) {
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();

        if ('N' == "N") {

            var data = { id: '495' + '~' + CycleId + '~' + ChangeNumber + '~' + DepositId, employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '37', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection }
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowDepositDetails")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DirectDetail", data: data, type: "POST" })
               .SetWidth(650)
               .SetHeight('60%')
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetTitle("Edit Direct Deposit Deduction")
        .SetonClose(function (e) {
            stopSpinner();
            var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            grid.dataSource.read();
        });

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

        }
        else {

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowDepositDetails")
   .SetIsModal(true)
   .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/ViewDirectDepositDetail?" + "id=" + '495' + '~' + CycleId + '~' + ChangeNumber + '~' + DepositId + '~' + 'N' })
               .SetWidth(650)
               .SetHeight('60%')
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetTitle("View Direct Deposit Deduction")
        .SetonClose(function (e) {
            stopSpinner();
            var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            grid.dataSource.read();
        });

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

        }

    }

    $("#btnEditAll__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').click();
        }

        selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        //debugger;
        if (typeof selectedRowId != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowId != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowId.length &gt; 0) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            var passValue = selectedRowId.split(',');

            var firstRecord = passValue[0];

            var data = { id: 0, employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '37', fromEditAll: true, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection }
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowDepositDetails")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DirectDetail", data: data, type: "POST" })
               .SetWidth(650)
               .SetHeight('60%')
               .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
               .SetTitle("Edit Direct Deposit Deduction")
               .SetonClose(function (e) {
                   onCloseDirectDepositDetailsPopup(e);
               });
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        }
    });

    function onCloseDirectDepositDetailsPopup(e) {
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }

    $("#btnEdit__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!$("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        if (selectedRowIds == "-1") {
            $('#btnEditAll__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').click();
            return;
        }

        var data = { id: 0, employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '37', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection }

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowDepositDetails")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DirectDetail", data: data, type: "POST" })
               .SetWidth(650)
               .SetHeight('60%')
                .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                .SetTitle("Edit Direct Deposit Deduction")
                .SetonClose(function (e) {
                    stopSpinner();
                    var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();
                });

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    $("#btnView__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {

    $("#btnDelete__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        if ($("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {

            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected record?", DeleteDirectDeposit);
        }
    });

    function DeleteDirectDeposit() {
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DeleteDirectDepositPopup',
            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                    var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/FixedAmountDetail", data: data, type: "POST" })
               .SetWidth('75%')
               .SetHeight('92%')
               .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
               .SetTitle("Add Fixed Amount Deduction")
               .SetonClose(function () {
                   stopSpinner();
                   var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                   grid.dataSource.read();
               })
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    });

    $("#btnEditAll__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView').click();
        }

        selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowId != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowId != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowId.length &gt; 0) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            var passValue = selectedRowId.split(',');

            var firstRecord = passValue[0];

            var data = { id: 0, employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '37', fromEditAll:true, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection }
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowFixedAmountDetails")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/FixedAmountDetail", data: data, type: "POST" })
               .SetWidth('75%')
               .SetHeight('92%')
               .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
               .SetTitle("Edit Fixed Amount Deduction")
               .SetonClose(function (e) {
                   onCloseFixedAmountDetailsPopup(e);
               });

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        }
    });

    function onCloseFixedAmountDetailsPopup(e) {
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }

    $("#btnEdit__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (selectedRowIds == "-1") {
            $('#btnEditAll__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView').click();
            return;
        }

        if (!$("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        var data = { id: 0, employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '37', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection }

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowFixedAmountDetails")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/FixedAmountDetail", data:data, type:"POST" })
                .SetWidth('75%')
                .SetHeight('92%')
                .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                .SetTitle("Edit Fixed Amount Deduction")
                .SetonClose(function (e) {
                    stopSpinner();
                    var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();
                });

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    $("#btnView__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

    $("#btnDelete__EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").click(function () {

        if ($("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {

            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected record?", DeleteFixedDeduction);
        }

    });

    function DeleteFixedDeduction() {

        $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DeleteFixedAmountPopup',
            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {

                //refresh grid

                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                    var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentFixedAmountDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    $("#btnSave__PayrollEmployeeDeduction").click(function (e) {
        $("#ApproveDeductionSet").val(false);
        SaveDeduction(e);
    });

    $("#btnSaveAndApprove__PayrollEmployeeDeduction").click(function (e) {
        $("#ApproveDeductionSet").val(true);
        SaveDeduction(e);
    });

    function SaveDeduction(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
        var form = $("#FormPayrollEmployeeDeduction");
        form.validate();
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if(result.Success)
                {
                    if(495 &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; 'True' == 'True')
                    {
                        if($("#ApproveDeductionSet").val() == 'true' &amp;&amp; '' != '')
                        {
                            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            var Id = result.Id;
                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DetailPopup",data:{id:'', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, sourceDataView:'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView'},type:"POST"});
                            var grid = $("#"+'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                            if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                                grid.dataSource.read();}
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success",  "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                            var grid = $("#"+'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                            if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                                grid.dataSource.read();}
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        var Id = result.Id;
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DetailPopup",data:{id:Id,sourceDataView:'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView'},type:"POST"});
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeePayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                            grid.dataSource.read();}
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success",  "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDetails_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    $("#btnAdd__PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        OpenAddEditPopup('Add');
    });

    $("#btnEdit__PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        OnEditOverrideGroupCap();
    });

    function OnEditOverrideGroupCap() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowId)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        if (typeof selectedRowId != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowId != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowId.length &gt; 0) {
            OpenAddEditPopup('Edit', selectedRowId);
        }
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    }

    $("#btnDelete__PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        if ($("#divPayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {

            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected item(s)?", DeleteOverrideGroupCap);
        }
    });

    $("#btnEditAll__PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView').click();
        }
        OnEditOverrideGroupCap();
    });

    function EditOverrideGroupCap(Id) {
        OpenAddEditPopup('Edit', Id);
    }

    function DeleteOverrideGroupCap() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        $("#divPayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DeleteDeductionOverrideGroupCap",
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    var grid = $("#PayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function OpenAddEditPopup(operation, deductionCapGroupId) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var url;
        if (operation == 'Add') {
            url = '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/CreateOverrideGroupCap';
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("PayrollOverrideGroupCapPopup")
                    .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: url, data: { employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '37' } })
                    .SetIsModal(true)
                    .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                    .SetTitle('Add Group Cap Override').SetWidth(750).SetIsResizable(false);
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PayrollDeductionCapGroupDetails", "PayrollDeductionCapGroupDetails", null);
        }
        if (operation == 'Edit') {
            url = "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DeductionOverrideGroupCap" + "?Id=" + deductionCapGroupId;

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("PayrollOverrideGroupCapPopup")
                         .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: url, data: $("#divPayrollOverrideGroupCapDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection() })
                         .SetIsModal(true).SetTitle("Edit Group Cap Override").SetWidth(750)
                    .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                    .SetIsResizable(false);
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PayrollDeductionCapGroupDetails", "PayrollDeductionCapGroupDetails", null);
        }
    }

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }
        
    })

<script>

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabelDirect").click(function () {

            var Id = $("#hdnMaskedValue_SSNLabelDirect").val();
            var buttonText = $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabelDirect").text();
            var showValue = buttonText.indexOf("(Show)") &gt; -1;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/QAAutom/AptaFundBase/ShowMaskedValue",
                data: {
                    ControlType: 'SSN', Id: Id, showValue: showValue
                },
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'json',
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                },
                success: function (response) {
                    if (response.Success == true) {
                        if ('SSN' != 'VendorTaxId') {
                            $("#lblSSNValue_SSNLabelDirect").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#lblVendorTaxIdValue_SSNLabelDirect").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabelDirect").text(response.buttonText);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });


</script>

<script>

    var saveInProgress = 0;
    var cntDepositLeft = 0;
    var cntDepositRight = 0;

    $("#btnSave__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        clearAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem();
        var primary = $('#PrimaryAllocation').val();
        var amount = $('#Amount').data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        var percent = $('#Percent').data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        if (primary == 'true' &amp;&amp; (percent &gt; 0 || amount &gt; 0)) {
            showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem("A percentage or amount cannot be specified for the primary direct deposit bank account.", "error")
            return;
        }
        else if (primary == 'false' &amp;&amp; (percent == null || percent == 0) &amp;&amp; (amount == null || amount == 0)) {
            showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem("Please enter percentage or amount to proceed with direct deposit.", "error")
            return;
        }
        if (saveInProgress == 0) {
            saveInProgress = 1;
            validateDirectDepositItem();
        }
        //$("#FormPayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDeposit").submit();
    });

    function closeDirectDepositItemWindow() {
        var grid = $("#EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
        $("#popupWindowDepositDetails").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

    function showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem(message, type) {
        clearAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem();
        if (type == "success") {
            ShowAjaxMessage(message, "success", "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDetail_Error");
        }
        else {
            ShowAjaxMessage(message, "error", "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDetail_Error");
        }

    }

    function clearAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
    }

    function validateDirectDepositItem(saveAndAdd, saveAndNext) {
        var form = $("#FormPayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDeposit");
        form.validate();
        var succMessage = 'Record saved successfully.';
        if ('' != "")
            succMessage = '' + ' saved successfully.';

        if (!form.valid())
            return;

        var data = form.serialize();
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            type: "POST",
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    if (saveAndAdd) {

                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        var data = { id: '-1', employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '0', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection}
                        $("#popupWindowDepositDetails").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DirectDetail", data: data, type: "POST" });
                        ShowAjaxMessage(succMessage, "success","PayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDetail_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else if (saveAndNext) {

                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        var data = { id: '', employeeID: '495', changeNumber: '0', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection}
                        $("#popupWindowDepositDetails").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployeeDeduction/DirectDetail", data: data, type: "POST" })
                            ShowAjaxMessage(succMessage, "success","PayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDetail_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDetail_Error");
                        closeDirectDepositItemWindow();
                    }
                }
                else {
                    saveInProgress = 0;
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PayrollEmployeeDeductionDirectDetail_Error");
                    $('btnSave__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView').prop('disabled', false);
                }
            }
        });

    }

    $("#btnCancel__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        closeDirectDepositItemWindow();
    });


    $("#btnSaveAndAdd__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        clearAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem();
        var primary = $('#PrimaryAllocation').val();
        var amount = $('#Amount').data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        var percent = $('#Percent').data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        if (primary == 'true' &amp;&amp; (percent &gt; 0 || amount &gt; 0)) {
            showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem("A percentage or amount cannot be specified for the primary direct deposit bank account.", "error")
            return;
        }
        else if (primary == 'false' &amp;&amp; (percent == null || percent == 0) &amp;&amp; (amount == null || amount == 0)) {
            showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem("Please enter percentage or amount to proceed with direct deposit.", "error")
            return;
        }
        validateDirectDepositItem(true);
    });

    $("#btnSaveAndNext__EmpPyDedAssignmentDirectDepositDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        clearAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem();
        var primary = $('#PrimaryAllocation').val();
        var amount = $('#Amount').data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        var percent = $('#Percent').data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        if (primary == 'true' &amp;&amp; (percent &gt; 0 || amount &gt; 0)) {
            showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem("A percentage or amount cannot be specified for the primary direct deposit bank account.", "error")
            return;
        }
        else if (primary == 'false' &amp;&amp; (percent == null || percent == 0) &amp;&amp; (amount == null || amount == 0)) {
            showAjaxMessageDirectPopupItem("Please enter percentage or amount to proceed with direct deposit.", "error")
            return;
        }
        validateDirectDepositItem(false, true);
    });


</script>

            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

<script>
    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }
        
    })
